[  308s] SoftHSM has been configured to store sensitive data in non-page RAM
[  308s] (i.e. memory that is not swapped out to disk). This is the default and
[  308s] most secure configuration. Your system, however, is not configured to
[  308s] support this model in non-privileged accounts (i.e. user accounts).
[  308s] 
[  308s] You can check the setting on your system by running the following
[  308s] command in a shell:
[  308s] 
[  308s] 	ulimit -l
[  308s] 
[  308s] If this does not return "unlimited" and you plan to run SoftHSM from
[  308s] non-privileged accounts then you should edit the configuration file
[  308s] /etc/security/limits.conf (on most systems).
[  308s] 
[  308s] You will need to add the following lines to this file:
[  308s] 
[  308s] #<domain>	<type>		<item>		<value>
[  308s] *		-		memlock		unlimited
[  308s] 
[  308s] Alternatively, you can elect to disable this feature of SoftHSM by
[  308s] re-running configure with the option "--disable-non-paged-memory".

[  308s] SoftHSM.
